    { 8359;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table14000981;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintBlankForm AND
                                  ("Export Document".GETFILTERS = '')
                               THEN
                                 ERROR(Text001);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ExportDocValidation@1240030000 : Record 14000985;
                                  Country@1240030002 : Record 9;
                                  x@1240030001 : Integer;
                                  Text1@1240030003 : Text[50];
                                BEGIN
                                  IF PrintBlankForm THEN
                                    EXIT;

                                  CLEAR(FinalConsignee);

                                  ShipperAddress[1] :=
                                    "PPI Name" + ', Attn: ' + "PPI Contact First Name" + ' ' + "PPI Contact Last Name";
                                  ShipperAddress[2] := "PPI Address";
                                  x := 3;

                                  IF "PPI Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    ShipperAddress[x] := "PPI Address 2";
                                    x := x + 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF "PPI State" <> '' THEN
                                    ShipperAddress[x] := "PPI City" + ', ' + "PPI State" + ', US'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShipperAddress[x] := "PPI City" + ', US';

                                  IF "Export Document"."Alt. Ult. Consignee" THEN BEGIN
                                    IF "Ult. Consig. Contact" <> '' THEN
                                      FinalConsignee[1] := "Ult. Consig. Name" + ', Attn: ' + "Ult. Consig. Contact"
                                    ELSE
                                      FinalConsignee[1] := "Ult. Consig. Name";
                                    FinalConsignee[2] := "Ult. Consig. Address";
                                    x := 3;

                                    IF "Ult. Consig. Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := "Ult. Consig. Address 2";
                                      x := x + 1;
                                    END;

                                    FormatAddress.FormatPostCodeCity(
                                      FinalConsignee[x],Text1,"Ult. Consig. City","Ult. Consig. ZIP Code","Ult. Consig. State",
                                      "Ult. Consig. Country Code");

                                    x := x + 1;
                                    IF Country.GET("Ult. Consig. Country Code") THEN
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := Country.Name
                                    ELSE
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := "Ult. Consig. Country Code";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    IF "Ship-to Contact" <> '' THEN
                                      FinalConsignee[1] := "Ship-to Name" + ', Attn: ' + "Ship-to Contact"
                                    ELSE
                                      FinalConsignee[1] := "Ship-to Name";

                                    FinalConsignee[2] := "Ship-to Address";
                                    x := 3;

                                    IF "Ship-to Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := "Ship-to Address 2";
                                      x := x + 1;
                                    END;

                                    FormatAddress.FormatPostCodeCity(
                                      FinalConsignee[x],Text1,"Ship-to City","Ship-to ZIP Code","Ship-to State","Ship-to Country Code");

                                    x := x + 1;
                                    IF Country.GET("Ship-to Country Code") THEN
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := Country.Name
                                    ELSE
                                      FinalConsignee[x] := "Ship-to Country Code";
                                  END;

                                  IF NOT "Alt. Sold-to" THEN
                                    Importer[2] := '  Same as ULTIMATE CONSIGNEE'
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                    IF "Sold-to Contact" <> '' THEN
                                      Importer[1] := "Sold-to Name" + ', Attn: ' + "Sold-to Contact"
                                    ELSE
                                      Importer[1] := "Sold-to Name";

                                    Importer[2] := "Sold-to Address";
                                    x := 3;

                                    IF "Sold-to Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      Importer[x] := "Sold-to Address 2";
                                      x := x + 1;
                                    END;

                                    FormatAddress.FormatPostCodeCity(
                                      Importer[x],Text1,"Sold-to City","Sold-to ZIP Code","Sold-to State","Sold-to Country Code");

                                    x := x + 1;
                                    IF Country.GET("Sold-to Country Code") THEN
                                      Importer[x] := Country.Name
                                    ELSE
                                      Importer[x] := "Sold-to Country Code";
                                  END;

                                  IF "Export Document"."Frt. Fwdr. Name" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    FrtFwdr[1] := "Frt. Fwdr. Name";
                                    FrtFwdr[2] := "Frt. Fwdr. Address";
                                    x := 3;

                                    IF "Frt. Fwdr. Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      FrtFwdr[x] := "Frt. Fwdr. Address 2";
                                      x := x + 1;
                                    END;

                                    FormatAddress.FormatPostCodeCity(
                                      FrtFwdr[x],Text1,"Frt. Fwdr. City","Frt. Fwdr. ZIP Code","Frt. Fwdr. State",
                                      "Frt. Fwdr. Country Code");

                                    x := x + 1;
                                    IF Country.GET("Frt. Fwdr. Country Code") THEN
                                      FrtFwdr[x] := Country.Name
                                    ELSE
                                      FrtFwdr[x] := "Frt. Fwdr. Country Code";
                                  END;

                                  IF "Related Companies" THEN
                                    RelatedX := 'X'
                                  ELSE
                                    NotRelatedX := 'X';

                                  IF "Hazardous Cargo" THEN
                                    HazardX := 'X'
                                  ELSE
                                    NotHazardX := 'X';

                                  IF "Routed Transaction" THEN
                                    RoutedX := 'X'
                                  ELSE
                                    NotRoutedX := 'X';


                                  IF ExportDocValidation.GET(ExportDocValidation.Table::"Transport Mode",0,"Mode of Transportation")
                                  THEN
                                    TransportationMethod := ExportDocValidation.Description;

                                  ExportDocValidation.SETRANGE(Table,ExportDocValidation.Table::"IATA/SCAC");
                                  ExportDocValidation.SETRANGE(Code,Carrier);
                                  IF ExportDocValidation.FIND('-') THEN
                                    CarrierName := ExportDocValidation.Description;
                                  ExportDocValidation.SETRANGE(Table,ExportDocValidation.Table::License);
                                  ExportDocValidation.SETRANGE(Code,"License Type");
                                  IF ExportDocValidation.FIND('-') THEN
                                    ExportLicense := ExportDocValidation.Description;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No. }

    { 1976;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table14000983;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Export Document No.,Type,No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF PrintBlankForm THEN
                                    EXIT;

                                  IF Type IN [Type::Item, Type::Resource] THEN BEGIN
                                    TempExportSourceLine := "Export Source Line";
                                    TempExportSourceLine.INSERT;
                                    LineFound := TRUE;
                                    IF "Export Control Class No." <> '' THEN
                                      ECCN := "Export Control Class No.";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Export Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 8762;    ;DataItem;SummarizeItems      ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempExportSourceLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Export Document No.",Type,"No.");
                               IF TempExportSourceLine.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                                 REPEAT
                                   NumberOfLines := NumberOfLines + 1;
                                 UNTIL TempExportSourceLine.NEXT = 0;
                                 TempExportSourceLine.FIND('-');
                                 TempPrevExportSourceLine := TempExportSourceLine;
                               END;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,NumberOfLines);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF PrintBlankForm THEN
                                    EXIT;

                                  IF TempExportSourceLine."No." <> TempPrevExportSourceLine."No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TempItemSummary := TempPrevExportSourceLine;
                                    TempItemSummary."Value USD" := TotalPrice;
                                    TempItemSummary."Weight (KGS)" := TotalWeight;
                                    TempItemSummary.INSERT;
                                    TempPrevExportSourceLine := TempExportSourceLine;
                                    TotalPrice := TempExportSourceLine."Value USD";
                                    TotalWeight := TempExportSourceLine."Weight (KGS)";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    TotalPrice := TotalPrice + TempExportSourceLine."Value USD";
                                    TotalWeight := TotalWeight + TempExportSourceLine."Weight (KGS)";
                                  END;

                                  IF TempExportSourceLine.NEXT = 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    TempItemSummary := TempPrevExportSourceLine;
                                    TempItemSummary."Value USD" := TotalPrice;
                                    TempItemSummary."Weight (KGS)" := TotalWeight;
                                    TempItemSummary.INSERT;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 3955;    ;DataItem;PrintSummaryItemLines;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempItemSummary.SETCURRENTKEY("Export Document No.",Type,"No.");
                               NumberOfLines := 0;

                               IF TempItemSummary.FIND('-') THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   NumberOfLines := NumberOfLines + 1;
                                 UNTIL TempItemSummary.NEXT = 0;

                               IF PrintBlankForm THEN
                                 SETRANGE(Number,1,1)
                               ELSE
                                 SETRANGE(Number,1,NumberOfLines);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  x@1240030000 : Integer;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF PrintBlankForm THEN
                                    EXIT;

                                  IF OnLine = 0 THEN
                                    TempItemSummary.FIND('-')
                                  ELSE
                                    TempItemSummary.NEXT;

                                  OnLine := OnLine + 1;
                                  CommodityCode := '';

                                  IF TempItemSummary."Schedule B Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    x := 1;
                                    WHILE x <= STRLEN(TempItemSummary."Schedule B Code") DO BEGIN
                                      IF x IN [5,7] THEN
                                        CommodityCode := CommodityCode + '.';
                                      CommodityCode := CommodityCode + COPYSTR(TempItemSummary."Schedule B Code",x,1);
                                      x := x + 1;
                                    END;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
